For this reason, this association has specially established temporary domestic goods markets in various districts based on the outline of work. After a long period of preparation and the enthusiastic participation of various factories, everything is almost ready. The opening is scheduled for the 14th. I still ask all sectors to give guidance in order to correct shortcomings." Then Huang Bingpei gave a speech, which is omitted.

Decisions on Various Cases

(1) Regarding the case of drawing lots for ordinary shop spaces and participating factory shop spaces, it was decided to draw lots on the spot.

(2) Regarding the case of stipulating business hours for the commercial center, it was decided that the market would open at 8:00 AM and close at 8:00 PM.

(3) Regarding the case of insurance for goods displayed by participating manufacturers, it was decided that the commercial center would negotiate with an insurance company, consolidate the insurance amounts required by each manufacturer, and jointly insure them. The amount of the premium would be distributed equally among the manufacturers based on the insured amount.

(4) Regarding the case of manufacturers hanging flags at their shop spaces, it was decided that no factory would be allowed to hang flags in the corridors of the commercial center's public roads, but they could do so at their entrances as they pleased.

Commercial Center Arrangement

The commercial center is located at the original site of the St. George Dance Hall at the intersection of Jing'an Temple Road and Yuyuan Road. No ceremony was held during the opening. Three electric light arches were erected at the main entrance of the tram station. One of the arches on each side had the words "Everyday National Goods, Everything You Need," and the other had "Exquisite Products, Dazzling Array." The shop spaces in the middle of the commercial center were for participating manufacturers, and the exhibition rooms were on both sides.

Dispute Over Inheritance After the Death of Famous Doctor Qin Heqi; Four Siblings Attack Each Other; Both Sides Attempt Reconciliation

The late famous trauma doctor Qin Heqi of Chuansha was fond of women during his lifetime. In addition to his legal wife, Mrs. Gu, he also married Mrs. Zhang, and later took two concubines, Mrs. Chen and Mrs. Xia. In total, he had four concubines and eleven children. Mrs. Gu gave birth to two daughters, who were married off long ago, one to the Cai family and the other to the Zhang family. Mrs. Zhang gave birth to five children: Meifang, Lingou, Rulin, Dongxin, and Zhenkun. Mrs. Chen gave birth to three children: Zhisheng, Zhiying, and Cici. Mrs. Xia only gave birth to one son, Zhiren. Heqi, because he believed that his elder brother Helou had no descendants, adopted his eldest son, Meifang, as his brother's son. However, Meifang and his elder sister, Lingou, colluded with each other. Seeing that their father's concubines were constantly giving birth to children, they feared that the number of people sharing their father's inheritance would increase day by day. In previous years, they secretly took their father's hidden title deeds to real estate and mortgaged them to others without authorization. Heqi discovered this and accused Meifang of disobedience at the Chuansha County Government. Although the court ordered Meifang to return the deeds, he never complied with the judgment. However, Heqi, due to the father-son relationship, was unwilling to strictly pursue the matter. On April 26th of last year, Heqi passed away. Meifang and his sister Lingou again seized all the title deeds to the inherited houses, land, and fifty or sixty mu of farmland in Chuansha, disregarding the interests of their other siblings. At that time, Mrs. Chen and Mrs. Xia sued them in the First Special District Court for seizing the inheritance. Because the two daughters born to Heqi's legal wife, Mrs. Gu, were already married to the Cai and Zhang families, or were close to Meifang, they specially listed the two daughters and Meifang Lingou as defendants. At that time, Meifang was deeply afraid that once the court heard the case, each person would be summoned to court, and cross-examination would be unfavorable to him. Therefore, he immediately sought reconciliation with Mrs. Chen and Mrs. Xia. All negotiations were not discussed with the two sisters, Cai Qin and Zhang Qin, who were also defendants. Later, after a settlement was reached and a contract was signed, Cai Qin and Zhang Qin should have signed the contract, but Meifang Lingou fraudulently signed on their behalf. It was not until recently that the two sisters learned of this. They negotiated with Meifang and others, but failed to reach a satisfactory solution. Therefore, they hired a lawyer to file a criminal self-accusation against Meifang Lingou, accusing the two defendants of encroaching on the inheritance and forging signatures, and requesting that they be investigated and dealt with according to law. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Risheng heard the case in court. The four siblings appeared in court, attacking each other and refusing to yield. The affection between siblings was replaced by the hostility of enemies. After Judge Huang investigated the facts with both parties, he advised them to go outside and try to reconcile. The case was granted an extension for further deliberation.

Tragic Murder on a Mahjong Table; A Fellow Mahjong Player Suddenly Opens Fire; Water Patrol Team Detective Captain Dies a Tragic Death; —One Suspect Arrested After Pursuit by Detectives—

Zhu Zifan, a native of Pudong, was 32 years old. He previously served as the captain of the anti-smuggling team of the Water Patrol Team. He was very capable in his work. Last year, he solved many theft cases and killed a notorious bandit named Mao Muxiang. Therefore, he was highly valued by his superiors. This spring, he was transferred to the Pudong Nanhui County to serve as the captain of the detective team of the Water Patrol Team. Due to official business, he often crossed the Huangpu River to Shanghai. The Huibao Hotel at No. 13, Lane 369, Guangdong Road, was his usual residence. Yesterday morning, Zhu came to Shanghai again on official business. He arrived at the port at 2:00 PM and immediately went to Room 6 of the Huibin Hotel to rest. Feeling bored, he invited his friend, Mr. Xu, who worked at the Japanese-owned Longhe Foreign Firm, and two unfamiliar travelers in the hotel to play mahjong in the parlor. Around 7:00 PM in the afternoon, two more travelers resembling workers suddenly arrived at the hotel and checked in. One was wearing a black cloth shirt and pants, claiming to be named Wang Jinshan, and the other was wearing blue cloth shirt and pants, named Chen Jinshan. The hotel clerk led them to Room 23 upstairs to stay. Unexpectedly, the two stayed in the room for a moment and then went downstairs together to watch the game. They also observed the game from the sidelines, which was a common occurrence and did not attract attention. Before long, the mahjong game ended, and the two unfamiliar guests who had been playing with Zhu announced their retirement. Zhu and others, feeling unsatisfied, casually asked if anyone else wanted to join the game. The two men on the side immediately agreed and joined the game again. Unexpectedly, Zhu's luck was very good. A round had barely passed when the outcome was immediately visible. While they were shuffling the tiles, the two men sitting to Zhu's left and right suddenly stood up and reached into their pockets. They told Zhu to slowly arrange the tiles. Zhu thought they were taking out money, so he did not suspect anything. But in an instant, what appeared before his eyes were two guns, aimed at Zhu's head. Mr. Xu, who was sitting opposite Zhu, knew something was wrong when he saw this and quickly turned around and ran outside. At the same time, gunshots rang out in the parlor, three in total. Two hit Zhu's forehead, and one hit his right chest. Immediately, blood spurted out, brains flowed out, and he fell backward. The two murderers, seeing that their goal had been achieved, quickly ran out of the alley to escape. The hotel staff also quickly chased after them and saw the two murderers reach the alley entrance. They shouted loudly, "Robbery!" The Chinese constable guarding the alley heard the sound and saw the two men running towards Shilu Road in a panic. Knowing that they were the criminals, he also assisted in the pursuit. Fortunately, the constables on duty had already received the news. When they saw the two murderers running towards them, they immediately drew their guns and ordered them to stop. One of the murderers, seeing the opportunity, turned around and fled into a nearby alley. One murderer was captured alive by the constables on duty, and a gun with several bullets was found on his body. He was immediately escorted to the Laozha Police Station for detention. At the same time, detectives were dispatched to the scene of the incident to investigate, and the injured Zhu Zifan was rushed to the hospital for treatment. Unfortunately, the injuries were fatal, and he died on the way. His body was transferred to the coroner's office for examination. The escaped murderer has been notified to all police agencies in the city to assist in the pursuit. As for the reason for Zhu Zifan's murder, it is said that it may be related to the killing of the notorious bandit Mao Muxiang. At the same time, whether the names and addresses filled in by the murderers at the hotel are their real names remains to be investigated. According to what they said, both are named Jinshan and both are 31 years old, which is quite suspicious.

Demanding Money by Holding a Dead Child; Spilling Wash Water Causes Trouble; Why Continue to Harass After Compensation Has Been Paid?

Mrs. Gu Wu, a woman from Pujiang, who lives at No. 118, Shengsheng Lane, Qianjiatang, French Concession, was washing her face on the morning of the [day left blank] of this month. When she poured the water out of the window, she accidentally splashed water on the four-year-old daughter, Baozhong, of Mrs. Zhang Liu, a Tianjin woman (named Wen [character left blank], 32 years old), who lives in the front parlor downstairs. The child seemed to be suffering from heat rash and was feeling unwell. Because the water splashed on her head, she was frightened and developed a fever and chills. The child's mother, Zhang Liu, shouted for people to call Gu Wu to a teahouse to reason. After the patrolmen learned of this, they detained the four hooligans who had been called by Liu to the police station. After questioning by the police chief, each was fined one dollar and released. Zhang Liu, unable to obtain what she wanted from Wu, carried the child's body upstairs, intending to send it into [Mr.] Wu's room to extort money. At this point, Gu Wu, finding that there was no point in reasoning, reported the matter to the Foch Road Police Station. Detectives were dispatched to investigate and learned that Zhang Liu's daughter had indeed died of heat rash, which resembled smallpox. They also inquired about everything from the second landlord, Wei Wang, and carried the child's body to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Coroner's Office to await an examination by the Second Special Court today.

Corrupt Police Officer Sentenced; Seller of Red Pills Fined

Bian Songlin from Yangzhou, together with Feng Liansheng from Wuxi, carried a leather suitcase containing four bags of red pills, totaling 4,000 pills, intending to transport them to the interior. On the morning of the 29th of last month, at around 8:00 AM, while passing the iron shed gate at the intersection of Xinqiao Street and Minguo Road in the French Concession, they were inspected and arrested by Patrolman Ni Lianxue, No. 426, of the French Police Station. Because Bian requested leniency and help, the patrolman took them to Yuan Shang Lane nearby and colluded with the gatekeeper patrolman of the lane, Liu Lianyuan, to demand 30 dollars from Bian for their release. Because Bian had no cash on hand, he borrowed money at home and managed to gather only 20 dollars. He entrusted Feng Liansheng's nephew, Lu Qiaogen, to send the money. Ni and Liu, because the amount of money was different from what they requested, refused to help. Ni then took Feng and Lu, along with the suitcase of red pills, to the police station. Later, the detectives continued to arrest Bian and seized a smoking pipe and four smoking needles in Bian's home. They were sent to the Special Court for interrogation and detention. During the investigation at the police station, Bian confessed that Ni and Liu had colluded to demand bribes. The police station arrested the two patrolmen and handed them over to the Special Court to be prosecuted for violating the anti-smoking law and the crime of dereliction of duty under the criminal law. After the trial was concluded by Judge Wang Gangxu, the date was set for sentencing. The circumstances have been recorded in detail in this newspaper. Yesterday was the date of sentencing. The police station escorted the defendants to the court. Judge Wang took the seat in the Fifth Criminal Court and sentenced Bian Songlin to a fine of 300 dollars for possessing opium substitutes with the intention of using them for smoking. Feng Liansheng was sentenced to a fine of 40 dollars for assisting in possessing opium substitutes with the intention of using them for smoking. If the fines are commuted to imprisonment, each dollar will be converted into one day. Ni Lianxue was sentenced to one year of imprisonment for demanding bribes for conduct contrary to his duties. Liu Lianyuan was sentenced to eight months of imprisonment for assisting in demanding bribes for conduct contrary to his duties. Before the judgment is final, the number of days of pre-trial detention will be used to offset the imprisonment, with two days offsetting one day of imprisonment, or one day offsetting two dollars of fine. The 4,000 red pills, one smoking pipe, and four smoking needles were confiscated and burned. Lu Qiaogen was found not guilty. During the appeal period, Bian Songlin paid a guarantee of 500 dollars or a shop guarantee. Feng Liansheng and Lu Qiaogen were still released on the original guarantee. Ni Lianxue requested to be released on bail, and the court allowed him to pay a 5,000-dollar shop guarantee to be summoned at any time and suspended his detention. Liu Lianyuan was detained in the detention center pending instructions.

Special Item

Overview of the Work of the Beijing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration for the First Quarter of the 23rd Year (7)

(Economizing on Consumption) The consumption of each station is primarily based on oil and electricity. Recently, practical economies have been implemented, which are expected to save approximately six thousand yuan annually. For example, Wuxi Station has added electrical lights where they were lacking, removed excessive ones, and installed switches as appropriate. In addition, switches were installed for all employee residences outside the station, and monthly electricity usage was limited. The station master of that station, Li Guisheng, designed to replace gasoline lamps with electric lights in the freight yards and at the east and west branch roads, saving considerable expense, and was immediately commended to encourage this.

Suzhou Station originally relied on its own power generation, with a total cost of one thousand four hundred and forty yuan per month. Recently, a commercial power plant has been supplying electricity day and night. After consultations, the station connected to the commercial power plant to receive an equivalent amount of electricity, estimated to cost seven hundred and forty yuan per month, saving seven hundred yuan compared to the previous arrangement, or eight thousand four hundred yuan annually.

The commercial electricity used by Kunshan Station was originally priced at 4.4 jiao per kilowatt-hour. However, for three months in winter, due to extended hours, an additional 3.6 jiao was charged per kilowatt-hour. Recently, an agreement was reached to cancel the winter surcharge. Starting this year, for the three winter months, the Administration will provide a fuel allowance of 30 yuan per month, for a period of two years.

In addition, in terms of car services, there are plans to switch to domestically produced printing materials, self-repair ticket rolling machines, reduce stationery usage, make envelopes from waste paper, discontinue the use of gasoline lamps, and discontinue telephone lines that are not strictly needed. It is estimated that this will save more than ten thousand yuan annually.

Furthermore, regarding telegrams sent by various stations, some were not in line with the nature of telegraphing, while others described facts in excessive detail or were overly complex. This not only wasted electricity but also obstructed the lines. Therefore, measures were established to address this. Unless absolutely necessary, long-distance telephone calls should be used instead of sending telegrams. If a telegram must be sent, its content must be concise and appropriate, avoiding unnecessary length.

(Cancellation of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Road Rental Agreement) In November of the 19th year, this Administration leased 200 new 20-ton freight cars from the China Railway Vehicle Company for the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, establishing a contract with 18 articles. In December of the 21st year, the Ministry of Railways ordered its cancellation. Starting in August of the 22nd year, under the guidance of Secretary Liu, dispatched by the Ministry, negotiations were conducted with the company. After eight meetings, it was decided that this Administration would purchase 23 of the company's already-equipped cars for a price of 59,800 yuan (equivalent to 2,600 national currency yuan per car). The Administration would also purchase the company's car parts at its discretion, cancel the original contract, and establish seven articles for subsequent arrangements. Subsequently, three additional meetings were held, and three additional articles were added as attachments to the subsequent arrangements. The parts were valued at 16,600 national currency yuan. Starting from January 15th of the 23rd year, the car price and parts will be paid to the company in installments.

(Recovery of Real Estate) The Hangzhou City Station Northeast Postal Bureau has approximately 15 mu of land in front of the road, which was previously leased by the Hangzhou Municipal Government to build City Station Park. Later, the open space south of the station was expanded by this Administration to create a park, which was adjacent to City Station Park. The Hangzhou Municipal Government then requested that the park be merged under the unified management of this Administration. Staff were dispatched to take over, and gardeners were transferred from the Jiaxing Nursery to manage it. Furthermore, the Asia Petroleum Company leased land along the railway in Zhabei to build a warehouse. Due to rent increases, the warehouse was sold to this Administration for 1,700 yuan. After repairs, it was divided into twelve rooms and allocated for use as accommodation for train crew members. (To be continued)

Reading and Answering Questions

Discussion on Issues of Esperanto Learning (1)

We believe that the answer given by Mr. on April 28th to Mr. Xiong Zifo of Guangzhou regarding the issue of learning Esperanto is generally correct. However, after reading it, we feel that there are several points that still require supplementation and discussion. We will briefly state our humble opinions below for Mr. to correct. After strongly arguing for the necessity of learning Esperanto, Mr. also pointed out the fallacies of Esperanto's opponents. Opponents focus on the artificiality of Esperanto, ignoring the fact that the Esperanto movement is progressing. Therefore, Mr. says: "Understanding the Esperanto movement from the language itself will naturally not lead to correct conclusions." Yes, their fallacy lies on the one hand in ignoring the fact that the Esperanto movement matures along with the maturity of the entire new cultural movement, but the root of their opposition to "artificial language" lies in their use of the traditional idealistic linguistic perspective to measure Esperanto. Idealistic linguists attempt to seek the ultimate nature of language in a static state, resulting in the separation of language from social relations, treating it as a naturally occurring, isolated phenomenon. (Look! How fragmented they are in researching ancient sounds, infatuated with old bones, in order to escape reality!) They deny the "artificiality" of language, even denying the lawful development of language. But as Adam Smith said, "All languages are artificial." The emerging linguistics tells us that language is neither divinely bestowed nor naturally occurring, but is created by humans themselves in response to the needs of real life. The process of creating this language was not consciously realized by the humans who created it until humans began to use consciousness to control social life. Human language corresponds to the evolution of society and develops according to certain laws. Human society progresses from primitive tribal life to feudal society, to capitalist society, to socialist society: Language also correspondingly goes through the stages of primitive language, dialect, national language (national language), and finally, inevitably, world common language. Now is the era when capitalism is beginning to collapse. On the one hand, the languages of various nations have developed to the extreme, and at the same time, in the womb of capitalism, beside the national language, the embryo of the future social world common language has been conceived. But can capitalism complete the task of this world common language? It is absolutely impossible. This impossibility is determined by the contradictions of capitalism in the age of imperialism." And the future common language "will never be German, nor Great Russian, but completely another kind of language." This is the scientific basis of Esperanto in linguistics.

Naturally, the so-called "artificial" above, the so-called "artificiality of language," does not refer to the concoction of any individual, but rather to the collective creation of the masses who actually use this language. L. L. Zamenhof, the originator of Esperanto, said: "Individuals can only be originators, not creators," "I don't want to stipulate the entire vocabulary, I don't want to create the entire language from beginning to end according to my personal preferences," "everything else" should be created by human society and real life, just as we see in all natural languages." This is the best annotation of collective language creation. At that time, what Zamenhof gave to the masses was six articles of grammar and a limited vocabulary (only this point was created by Zamenhof's own hands and commonly followed by everyone as the "foundation of Esperanto"), and at the same time he declared the abandonment of all his personal privileges over this language, and entrusted this labor and its future growth entirely to the practical use of the masses. "Esperanto has no personal legislator, nor is it subordinate to any individual. All opinions and writings of the originator of Esperanto, like the opinions and writings of all other Esperantists, are of an absolutely private nature, and have no compulsory nature for anyone." Based on Zamenhof's wise and democratic principles, Esperanto is constantly collectively created by the international masses who actually use it (and are growing in size), gradually approaching perfection, and becoming the embryo of the future social common language.

Secondly, we believe that Mr.'s understanding of obtaining basic knowledge is too mechanical. A certain degree of basic knowledge is naturally necessary for new cultural movement activists. However, the path to obtaining this basic knowledge is not limited to mechanically reading a few books, but can have various different paths. Some people have entered this path from novels, while others have entered it from the screen or stage, and have begun to correctly understand the structure of this society. This is why literature, film, and theater, which have always been regarded as non-mass things, also have their full value and reason for existence in the field of mass cultural movement (of course, not to say that they are more noble than other departments, but also certainly not inferior). And if we know that the acquisition of basic knowledge should also be experienced and learned from real life, then why doesn't Esperanto, which can be used to penetrate into the real life of the international masses, have such value? Isn't Esperanto one of the good tools for acquiring basic knowledge? Here, it is very appropriate to quote the words of the Japanese Esperantist Akita Ujaku: "For all young men and women, I unconditionally recommend learning Esperanto. I am convinced that Esperanto is the gateway and guide for all young men and women to advance towards a correct worldview and a correct social view." (Luo Suofu Chen Jue Lai)

Chairman of the Games, Ladies and Gentlemen, I am extremely delighted to represent the China National Amateur Athletic Federation and the Chinese delegation in extending congratulations to the 10th Far Eastern Games. At today's meeting, in addition to all the athletes from the original three member countries since the establishment of the Far Eastern Games in 1913, we also have the participation of the Dutch East Indies. Mayor Wu of Shanghai has found an excellent location, and the funds of over one million yuan have also been raised and will soon be used to start construction. Although we already have a magnificent sports field in the capital, Nanjing, we still eagerly hope for a large sports field in Shanghai, because we feel that Shanghai is better able to host a large number of athletes from various countries. The value of promoting international sports need not be reiterated. I firmly believe that all the member countries that founded this Far Eastern Games will continue their loyalty and cooperation to the end. Finally, on behalf of the China National Amateur Athletic Federation, the Chinese delegation, and myself personally, I express my sincere gratitude to all the staff of the Philippine Amateur Athletic Federation and the people of the Philippines for the friendly hospitality they have shown us since our arrival in the Philippines.

Commemorative Stamps of the Games

Methods of Winning Championships — Women's Performances —

The competition regulations for the nine championships of the Far Eastern Games are as follows:

(1) Track and Field Events include high jump, long jump, triple jump, pole vault, 16-pound shot put, discus, javelin, a total of seven events. The top four in each event are awarded points based on 5-3-2-1.

(2) Track Events include 100 meters, 200 meters, 400 meters, 800 meters, 1500 meters, 10,000 meters, 110 meters hurdles, and 400 meters hurdles, a total of eight events. The top four in each event are awarded points based on 5-3-2-1.

(3) All-Around Events include 400-meter relay, 600-meter relay, pentathlon, decathlon, awarded points based on 16-4-2.

(4) Swimming includes 50-meter freestyle, 100-meter freestyle, 200-meter breaststroke, 100-meter backstroke, 400-meter freestyle, 1500-meter freestyle, and 200-meter relay. The top four in each event are awarded points. Except for the relay, which is calculated as 16-4-2, the rest are calculated as 5-3-2-1. Fancy diving is not scored and is for performance purposes only.

(5) Football adopts a single round-robin system, with each team playing each other once. The winner gets 2 points, a draw gets 1 point, and a loss gets 0 points. The team with the most points wins the championship. If the game is a draw, it will be extended for 15 minutes. If it is still a draw, our country advocates for a rematch, while Japan advocates splitting the championship. This issue has not yet been resolved. (6) Basketball adopts a double round-robin system, meaning each team must meet any opposing team twice. The winner is calculated based on percentage. If the scores are equal after the round-robin, a final will be held to determine the championship.

(7) Volleyball adopts a double round-robin system, meaning each team must meet any opposing team twice. The winner is calculated based on percentage. If the percentages are equal after the round-robin, a final will be held to determine the championship.

(8) Baseball adopts a double round-robin system, meaning each team must meet any opposing team twice. The winner is calculated based on percentage. If the percentages are equal after the round-robin, a final will be held to determine the championship.

(9) Tennis adopts the Davis Cup system, divided into four singles groups and one doubles group. Two singles players exchange matches once each with one player from the opposing team. Each group is best of five sets.

(10) Women's sports are all for performance purposes. This year there are only two events: tennis and volleyball. Our country has no hope in either. Volleyball is a round-robin system, and tennis is a Davis Cup system, but each group adopts the best of three sets.

Evaluation of the Nine Championships: Our Country Has Great Hopes in Football, Volleyball, and Tennis; The Philippine Army is Confident in Basketball, and Baseball is Also Ambitious; Track and Field, All-Around, and Swimming Will Be Controlled by Japan

The 10th Far Eastern Games, with athletes from China, Japan, the Philippines, and the Dutch East Indies gathering in the Philippines, is scheduled to open in Manila this afternoon at 2 PM. Since the abolition of the overall championship, the situation of each country has been concentrated under the individual championships, which will be described separately as follows:

Football Championship: Our Country Has Very High Hopes; Java is a Strong Enemy; Japan and the Philippines Claim to be Equals

First of all, in terms of football, the football championship was our country's exclusive possession before the 9th Games, except for the first Games, not allowing others to get involved. Since the last Games in Tokyo, when we drew with Japan, the Japanese ambition has since flourished. In terms of their technique, it is indeed better than in the past, but according to a special dispatch from five Japanese newspapers, our country's coach Huang Jiajun observed the Japanese team's practice and found that their technique is far inferior to our country's. Therefore, Japan's desire to win the football championship is a dream. And Java is our country's only strong enemy. Javanese players are accustomed to the tropics and have already gained a geographical advantage. However, it is rumored that five overseas Chinese players among them have said that they will not work for Java, with at most three of them doing so. If so, then our country has a firm grasp of the football championship. In addition, this time, generals Li Huitang and Feng Jingxiang are serving as forwards, and the offensive is stronger than in the previous Games, then the Japanese will be even less of a concern. As for the Philippines, gathering the essence of Manila and being the host team, its strength is actually not as weak as imagined.

Tennis Championship: Success or Failure Depends on Doubles; China and Japan Have Equal Hopes

This year's tennis championship, our country has the hope of restoring the glory of the 8th Games in 1928. Although Lin Baohua cannot go due to matters, Qiu Feihai, Xu Chengji, and Lin Wangsu are all the essence of our country. If they can eliminate Japan in the preliminary round, it is equivalent to winning the championship. Therefore, today's China-Japan tennis match is the final. Because the Javanese players have no one who can defeat Xu Chengji, and the Philippines relies entirely on Kavier alone. Although Kavier has improved, he is helpless in supporting a giant building with a single tree, and the hope is very slim. As for the situation between China and Japan, Sato Hyotaro and our country's Qiu Xu will have a fierce battle, and Yamada will definitely be able to win against Qiu Xu. If Qiu Xu's doubles can win, our country's championship is already in hand. The key to success or failure lies entirely in this.

Volleyball Championship: China and the Philippines Will Definitely Compete; Our Country Has Hope of Winning the Championship Again

After the Guangzhou volleyball players of our country went south together, the hope is also one of the greatest items. Java did not participate, and Japan is actually far behind. The final is really between China and the Philippines. This time, our country has combined the elites of Guangdong, Hong Kong, and Shanghai to form a strong team. The strength is really above the previous Games. The volleyball in the Philippines has indeed improved recently. The fierce competition between China and the Philippines is to be expected. However, our country will win against the Philippines eight or nine times out of ten. Therefore, when Chief Leader Wang Zhengting arrived in the Philippines, in his conversation, he also placed our country's hopes on volleyball.

Basketball Championship: The Philippines Has the Most Confidence; Our Country Only Hopes to Beat Japan

In the basketball championship, the situation is a three-legged rivalry, with the Philippines being dominant. This championship is also one of the ones that the Philippines has been striving for in previous Games. Its technology and ball skills are indeed unmatched by other countries. Therefore, the Philippines is still the most confident and hopeful. Since Japan suffered at our hands in the last Games, they have been complacent, which is chilling. Moreover, the last Games were held in Tokyo, and there were questions among the referees. This time, our country's players have also been gathered together for some time. Therefore, although there may not be a guarantee of defeating the Philippines in the future, we will definitely be able to defeat the enemy and win tonight when we first meet Japan. Java has also not participated in basketball.

Baseball Championship: The Philippines Rises as a New Force; Japan Should Not Be Too Optimistic

In the baseball item, our country is the most hopeless, but it is not discouraged or intimidated by the immaturity of the art. Therefore, although there were people who advocated not sending a baseball team before the event, it eventually became a re-engagement to respond to the spirit of this sport. Japan has possessed the baseball championship for several Games, but there is a great possibility of change this time. Japan's first-class pitcher Nakamura Mineo broke his ankle during practice and will not be able to take the field and show off his skills, which is a major blow to Japan. At the same time, the baseball strength of the Philippines should not be ignored. The reason for the Philippines' failure in the last Games was the inability to recruit first-class players. Because the good players in the Philippines are concentrated under the Philippine Baseball League, at that time, the Philippine Sports Association believed that the players under the league were all professional athletes and rejected them. But now it is different. The Philippine Sports Association has recognized the athletes under the league as amateur players. Therefore, this year, 20 good players will be selected from the league to compete against Japan. Japan's victory is not guaranteed. It is a pity that our compatriots in Honolulu cannot return to the country to serve, otherwise, the results would be satisfactory.

Track and Field, All-Around, and Swimming: To Be Handled by Japan; Our Country Has More Hope of Scoring Points

As for the four items of track and field, all-around, and swimming, they will undoubtedly fall into the hands of the Japanese. There is no doubt about it. If our athletes work hard, they may not be completely wiped out. Fu Baolu's pole vault and Liu Changchun's sprint both hold great hope. As for the Philippines, although they will definitely not score as many points as the Japanese in these four items, it is inevitable that they will pose a great threat to the Japanese. For example, in track and field, Torrebiva's high jump, Kamandi's shot put, Yeder's middle distance in track events, Garcia's high hurdles, and Alabur and White's middle hurdles are all masterpieces. The strengths of China, Japan, and the Philippines are equal in the 200 meters, which is especially feared by the Japanese. In the all-around, Philippine athlete Bard recently created a new record in the pentathlon, as well as the relay. The Filipinos will also not be willing to fall behind in swimming. For example, Irde Alfonso and Zikiram have both created world records. The Japanese are not allowed to be optimistic.

A Brief History of the Far Eastern Games

— Wei

(1) The Beginning Era

Before the 20th century, there were more than ten countries, large and small, on the coast of Asia, with hundreds of millions of people, each living and working in peace and contentment, with little interaction. There was even less to talk about in terms of sports. Since the Philippines became a colony of the United States, more and more Americans came to the Philippines to promote education. In 1911, under the advocacy and management of an American named Brown (Flwood S Bronr), the Philippine Sports Association was established. As such, the Far Eastern Sports Association also began.

Before the Far Eastern Sports Association was established, the Philippine Carnival was held every February. During the carnival, a grand sports meeting was always held. In the year of Xuantong 3 of the former Qing Dynasty, the Philippine Sports Association initiated an invitation to China and Japan to participate in the carnival in Manila, the capital of the Philippines. At that time, China sent track and field and football athletes to participate. Japan also sent two tennis players and a baseball team to attend. With this motivation, the Philippine Sports Association initiated the organization of the Far Eastern Sports Association and appointed Krone, Brown, and Tuttherly to form an organizing committee to preside over all preparatory matters.

(2) Brown's Efforts

In view of this trend, the Philippines further proposed to organize the Far Eastern Games, modeled after the World Games, initiated by China, Japan, and the Philippines. The Games would be held in major cities in East Asia every other year, with the aim of promoting the relations between the three countries and the sports of their citizens. In September of the first year of the Republic of China, Brown, on behalf of the Philippine Sports Association, officially visited China and Japan to propose the original plan and intention to organize the Far Eastern Sports Association. China and Japan felt that there was a similar need, so China first resolutely joined, and Japan also participated in an informal capacity. The first Games were held in Manila in February of the second year of the Republic of China during the Philippine Carnival. China officially sent athletes to the meeting. Because Japan's sports association was not yet fully organized at that time, it did not have the strength to send athletes, so it only sent a baseball team and two track and field athletes to attend. Because of the lack of detailed organization and regulations in various sports, it was not possible to achieve good results in that competition. The second Games were held in Shanghai, China. Talents from various countries greatly increased, so the results also improved a lot. Therefore, Japan declared that it would officially join the Games as a member country starting from the third Games. From then on, the foundation was firmly established, and all organizational outlines and competition rules were readily available.

(3) Aims and Objectives

The purpose of organizing the Far Eastern Games was to seek the great union of the countries of the Far East. Therefore, it was not considered satisfactory to have only two or three member countries join. After the closing of the first Games, Lang wanted to expand the organization of the Games, so he personally went to Bangkok, Siam, and Singapore to persuade Siam and Malaya to join. Although they all agreed to participate, unfortunately, the European War broke out, and the port was closed, so this proposal became a pipe dream. In the ninth year of the Republic of China, Brown, considering that the previous achievements had not been completed, traveled to India and Java again, still persuading them to participate. However, by the seventh Games, it was still not implemented. When the eighth Games were held in Shanghai, India sent a telegram wanting to participate. Our country replied with a welcome, but it was unsuccessful again due to events. It was not until the ninth Games held in Tokyo, Japan, that India sent athletes to participate in an unofficial capacity.

(4) Relationship with the Olympic Committee

Compared with the World Olympic Committee, the Far Eastern Sports Association is nothing more than an immature organization. Now the order of the Far Eastern Games is as far as possible in accordance with the Olympic Games, except for the special circumstances of each country not being included in this exception. All the rest have the same place. The current meeting period has been changed to once every four years, and it is conducted in the interim with the Olympic Games, so as to avoid conflicts in time.

The nature and relationship between the two associations are not contradictory and have a tendency to complement each other. Because the Olympic Committee has no conditions or restrictions on the Far Eastern Sports Association and does not infringe on its privileges, the Far Eastern Sports Association can therefore increase its reputation and influence. Moreover, the Olympic Committee sends one member as a special envoy to each Far Eastern Movement Meeting, and in the countries concerned, defines the famous athletes as the specialized representatives of the Olympic Committee, so as to guide the events of the Far Eastern Movement Meeting and promote the development of its affairs.

(5) Patronage of the World Sports Community

At the time of the establishment of the Far Eastern Sports Association, it was encouraged by Sloan, Ormous, and Wendell, American members of the Olympic Committee, and they gave a gold flower ring to the Far Eastern Games as a championship prize. However, the Olympic Committee did not officially recognize the Far Eastern Games until 1920. The reason for the long delay was the obstruction of the European War, not the disapproval or inattention to this new international organization. When the Olympic Committee held a regular meeting in Antwerp this year, Brown attended on behalf of the Far Eastern Sports Association, elaborating on the purpose and achievements of the Far Eastern Games. The members of all countries fully agreed and decided to send Kano Jigoro as the official of the Olympics

Track and Field

Representing and participating in the Fifth Far Eastern Games held in Shanghai in 1921, of the Far Eastern Committee within the Olympic Committee at that time, only Mr. Kano delivered a congratulatory speech on behalf of the Olympic Committee at the opening of the Fifth Far Eastern Games, explained the situation at the Antwerp Conference to the Far Eastern Games, and reported the results of the Shanghai meeting to Mr. Coubertin, the President of the Olympic Committee.

In the autumn of 1922, Count de Baillet-Latour (i.e., the current President) Vice-President of the Olympic Committee, served as a special envoy and went from Europe to America to participate in the First Latin American Games held in the Brazilian capital in September. He also planned to go to Osaka, Japan, to participate in the Sixth Far Eastern Games in May 1923. His trip to South America was quite busy. After the meeting, he planned to inspect the physical education situation in various countries. He originally planned to travel around the Far East and finally arrive in Osaka, Japan. Japan had also actively prepared to welcome him. However, when Mr. de Baillet-Latour was about to depart from the United States, he suddenly received a telegram and was recalled to Europe due to some matter, which resulted in his inability to make the trip. This was a great disappointment to the Far Eastern Games. Subsequently, Mr. Coubertin, the President of the Olympic Committee, expressed his hope that Dr. Wang Zhengting, a new member of the Olympic Committee, would represent the Olympic Committee at the Sixth Far Eastern Games. However, due to the tense diplomatic relations between China and Russia, Mr. Wang was also unable to attend, and Mr. Kano Jigoro, a Japanese member, represented the Olympic Committee and read a congratulatory telegram at the opening ceremony.

Baseball Field

(6) Contributions and Efforts of Chinese and Filipino People to the Far Eastern Games

The Far Eastern Athletic Association's ability to exist to this day must be attributed to the efforts of Mr. Brown. Former Philippine Governor-General Forbes and the late Governor-General Wood both provided great support for the organization and development of the Far Eastern Athletic Association. Others such as Quezon, Osias, Earnshaw of the Philippines, Crone, Marquardt, Tutheriy, England of the United States, and the late President Li Yuanhong, the late Foreign Minister Dr. Wu Tingfang, former Prime Minister Xiong Xiling, former Foreign Minister Tang Shaoyi, and the current Honorary President of the Chinese National Amateur Athletic Federation Dr. Wang Zhengting, and Chairman Dr. Zhang Boling, etc. of our country have made many efforts and contributions to the Far Eastern Games, which we must not forget.

(7) Japanese Obstruction and Sabotage of the Far Eastern Games

In the past twenty years, the Far Eastern Games have seemed to be progressing smoothly on the surface, but in fact, they have gone through many twists and turns, and each time it has been caused by the Japanese.

A. The Twenty-One Demands at the Second Games. The Second Far Eastern Games were held in Shanghai in 1915. At that time, Japan was making the Twenty-One Demands to our country, and the diplomatic relations between China and Japan were on the verge of breaking off. The Japanese public opinion circles criticized the Japan Athletic Association for not participating in the Far Eastern Games, but in the end, it was still decided to participate. When the Japanese athletes arrived in Shanghai, the Games had already been opened for two days. When the Japanese athletes entered the field and passed in front of the stands, they were spat upon by the audience, which almost caused a disaster. Fortunately, those in charge in our country understood the general situation and explained to the audience, so nothing happened. This was one of the twists and turns of the Far Eastern Games.

B. The Unreasonable Demand by the Japanese to Postpone the Fourth Games

In 1919, the Fourth Games were held in Manila. Unfortunately, a major wave suddenly occurred before the Games. Again, the Japanese complained and caused an unprecedented major problem for the Games. The reason for this incident stemmed from the Japan Athletic Association. The Japan Athletic Association believed that the Games period coincided with the school examination period and informed the Philippines, the country concerned, requesting that the Games period be postponed to August. The Philippine Athletic Association believed that August was the rainy season in the southern country and was not suitable for large-scale international games, and resolutely rejected Japan's unreasonable request. The Japan Athletic Association was embarrassed and angry, and suddenly announced that it would not send athletes to participate in the Games, and declared its permanent withdrawal from the Far Eastern Athletic Association. However, at this time, there was a great uproar in Japanese public opinion circles, and they opposed this move by Japanese athletics. The Japanese finally admitted that they were wrong and still participated in the Games. This was the second of the twists and turns of the Far Eastern Games.

C. The Japanese Athletes' Walkout at the Seventh Games. The Seventh Games were held in the Philippines in 1925. On the first day of the opening of the Games, the Japanese player Noto, whom the Japanese considered the most promising player in the 400-meter final, was disqualified. Thereupon, all the Japanese athletes protested together, and as a result, they all withdrew from the field. Fortunately, Philippine Governor-General Wood came forward to mediate, and thereupon the Japanese withdrew from track and field, but other competitions continued. This was the third of the twists and turns of the Far Eastern Games.

D. The Twists and Turns of Japanese Movement and the False State's Participation in this Games

In this Games, the Japanese disregarded world justice and used the puppet state they had established to demand to join the Games. During the Sino-Philippine Standing Committee meeting held in Shanghai, they made this unreasonable request. After being severely refuted by our country's representatives, the Japanese threatened to withdraw from the Games. As a result, they still knew they were wrong and still participated, and the Far Eastern Games escaped from the storm again. This was the fourth of the twists and turns of the Far Eastern Games.

(8) Future and Dangerous Transportation

Looking back at the twenty years since the Far Eastern Games were founded, up to now, all the past Games have been held, and the Japanese have obstructed them four times. China and the Philippines have always adhered to their original intentions and strongly supported and maintained the Games, while the Japanese have sabotaged them everywhere. Although this Games was fortunately opened, there are still many hidden reefs in the future. The puppet state is not qualified to attend the Games and is under the protection of the Japanese. It plans to organize the so-called "Asian Games," which are all harmful insects that destroy the Far Eastern Games. The next Games will be held in Shanghai, and everything will be presided over by our country, so there will be no problems. However, when the 12th Games are held, they will be hosted by the Japanese again. At this time, the issue of the puppet state's participation will definitely be revived, and the Japanese will definitely support its participation. At this time, if our country does not have a proper solution, it will inevitably withdraw from the Games.

Since our country fundamentally does not recognize the existence of the puppet state, we should find a way to fundamentally eliminate the puppet state. We hope that when the 12th Games are held in Tokyo, our country's government will have recovered the lost territory of Northeast China and the puppet state will no longer exist, so that our country's sports circles will not be troubled by this issue. Otherwise, if Japan allows the puppet state to join, we will withdraw in shame, and all countries in the world will laugh at our sports circles' lack of resistance.

Third Day of the Two Rivers Revival Anniversary

Today, the Two Rivers Women's Physical Education Normal School in Jiangwan, this city, is holding a student achievement exhibition. From 8:00 am, the public is welcome to attend and provide criticism and guidance throughout the day. The achievement exhibition is not divided into rooms and is all held in the school's auditorium. There are groups such as the basketball team's northern expedition to Pingjin, memorial prizes for the eastern expedition to Japan, memorial prizes for the southern expedition to Minyue, all-sports Games trophy prizes, Shanghai Western Youth Games, Chinese Women's Games, and International Women's Games trophy prizes. Other items on display include architectural methods, sports postures, and other patterns, as well as homework achievements in Chinese language, exercise physiology, and other subjects. In the afternoon, there will be basketball, tennis, and baseball games to entertain the audience.

Also, the concert yesterday attracted about 3,000 guests throughout the day, which was even more enthusiastic than the first day. All fourteen scenes of the program were performed with Western music, with clear singing voices and skilled techniques.

Education News

The Radical Progress of the Jiangxi Agricultural College: 50,000 Yuan in Funding, Divided into Five Departments

(Nanchang, 11th) The Jiangxi Agricultural College has an annual operating expense of 550,000 yuan and is divided into five departments: agriculture, economics, extension, plant production, animal production, and rural education. A large-scale experimental field is being built near Xishan, with equipment costs of 100,000 yuan, to carry out breeding, pest control, and the production of blood serum for the prevention and control of livestock diseases.

The Nanjing Municipal Social Affairs Bureau States that the Joint Examination Cannot Be Avoided, and Students Announce a Strike

(Nanjing, 11th) The principals of various private middle schools met with Wang Chongzhi, the Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, on the morning of the 11th regarding the joint examination. Director Wang was busy with official duties and sent Section Chief Qian to meet them instead. The students' eight demands were presented on behalf of the principals, and the social affairs authorities stated that it was impossible to waive the examination, but the questions could take into account the actual situation and be made slightly simpler. (Nanjing, 11th) Middle school students in Nanjing went on strike today to protest the joint examination and issued a declaration against the joint examination, which mainly included: 1. It violates the principles of education; 2. It restricts the development of students' talents; 3. It damages students' physical and mental health. It also stated that the joint examination has no practical value, the selection of questions for the joint examination is prone to losing focus, the treatment in the joint examination is unequal, and the effectiveness of the joint examination is a bird's-eye view. We earnestly request the education authorities to uphold their sincere love for students and withdraw the order for the joint examination. We will implement a strike from today to express our determination and awaken the authorities. We hope that compatriots across the country will provide substantial assistance.

Conflicts Also Occur at Pinghongda College

(Beiping, 11th) At Hongda College, students and the principal clashed this morning over the joint examination. The principal fired a gun to show his feelings. Fortunately, no misfortune occurred.

Director Pan of the Municipal Education Bureau Instructs on the Guiding Principles for Middle School Training Students

Yesterday, he convened a discussion with middle school principals and deans of students. The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau convened a discussion with middle school principals and deans of students in this city at the YMCA in Baxianqiao at 3:00 pm yesterday. More than 150 principals and deans of students from schools such as Hujiang Affiliated Middle School, Guanghua Affiliated Middle School, Daxia Affiliated Middle School, Aiguo, Wuben, Jingye, Junyi, McLaren, Zhonghua Vocational Education, Shanghai Middle School, Nanyang Middle School, Huadong Girls' Middle School, Pudong Middle School, Shanghai Girls' Middle School, Chengdong Girls' Middle School, East Asia Physical Education Teacher Training School, Aiqun, and Guangxia attended. More than 200 people, including Wei Ke, Chen Qun, Cao Huiqun, Lin Zhongke, Ni Wenya, Jia Botao, Jia Foru, Li Haoshan, Liao Maoru, Yan Zhenyu, Wang Xiaoying, and Shen Tilan, were present. Director Pan of the Municipal Education Bureau gave a speech, instructing on the guiding principles for middle schools to train students. Finally, Cao Huiqun, Liao Maoru, Chen Jicheng, Li Haoshan, Sun Letao, and others expressed their opinions. It lasted for more than two hours before it ended. The full text of Director Pan's speech is recorded below:

Today, the Municipal Education Bureau invited all middle school principals and deans of students in the city to exchange opinions and discuss several middle school issues. The number of public middle schools established in Shanghai is very small, accounting for less than 5% of the total. To make progress in middle school education in the city, we certainly cannot only look at the municipal middle schools. Moreover, due to the limited funds of the municipal government and various other factors such as location, manpower, and material resources, we can frankly admit that the number of municipal schools is small, and their quality is not necessarily better than that of private schools. Or, it can be said that there are many areas where they are not as good as private middle schools that have a long history and are well-run. Therefore, we believe that to enable Shanghai middle school students to receive a good education, public and private middle schools must exchange opinions and work together. Only then can middle school education in Shanghai have the possibility of upward progress. The reason why we invited everyone to participate in this meeting during a very busy time is nothing more than to take this opportunity to report to you the several things that the Education Bureau hopes to do for middle schools in Shanghai in the future. At the same time, we are also very willing to take this opportunity to hear from several gentlemen who are very interested in, very researched, and very experienced in middle school education, and to provide guidance on the main road that Shanghai middle schools should take in the future and the policies that should be adopted, so that teachers who run middle schools in the city can use them as a reference. Therefore, although this meeting has no resolution, if everyone agrees that the results of today's discussion are a road that should be taken and a policy that should be adopted, and that we are planning the best road for middle school students to run education, then middle school education will certainly achieve the purpose of development.

The most important key to the opinions that the Education Bureau wants to contribute is to first understand how Shanghai middle school education should be done in the future. Many people say that many disputes have occurred in universities in the past few years, and they are all blamed on university students, saying that they do not meet our ideals, or they are blamed on school administrators for not fulfilling their responsibilities. In fact, university problems are very complicated. From the perspective of educational administration, the management of higher education is naturally presided over by the Ministry of Education, and I believe that there are plans to improve the methods there. Therefore, our local educational administrative organs start by paying attention to middle schools first. However, if middle school students are well-trained, even if universities often have problems now, if many good middle school students enter universities in a few years, universities will gradually change. Therefore, it can be said that it is indirectly laying the foundation for university education. It is not that we are ignoring higher education, but in my personal opinion, the age of middle school students is a period of great change that can be either east or west, which is not comparable to the age of university students who have reached a considerable level of maturity. Therefore, middle school students should be absolutely led and managed by teachers and staff within the school. University students may have the ability to move automatically, and this issue is worth studying separately. As for middle school students, we do not deny that they have the ability to do extracurricular work or extracurricular activities. But I dare say that middle school students' extracurricular activities and extracurricular work must be guided by teachers and staff at all times, so that they can avoid being led to the right path. Because middle school students' knowledge and learning are still in the organizational stage, if there is no appropriate leadership, they will inevitably go astray. Therefore, the responsibility of middle school teachers and staff to students is actually even more important than that of university teachers and staff. I think everyone has the same feeling. However, the methods of each school are different in the past. Some tend to be strict, some are more laissez-faire, and the results are also different. Under this circumstance, we certainly cannot universally hope that Shanghai middle schools can create a kind of student. To achieve this hope, we must discuss more on training in order to move towards a common path. Therefore, the first point is that we hope that middle school principals and deans of students should help the Education Bureau, and the Education Bureau should help middle school principals and deans of students, and work together to complete this important mission of leading middle school students and training middle school students. In the future, middle school students' exploration of learning and extracurricular activities, the responsibility for leadership and training, completely rests on the teachers and staff, and should not let students act blindly, or say that students' movements or youth movements, the school does not allow him to move, for fear that students will object, or someone calls him to move, if he is not allowed to move, the person who calls him to move will object. Because of this suspicion and speculation, teachers and staff are unwilling to take more responsibility to guide students. In fact, we do not deny the ability of middle school students to act, but middle school students' activities must be under the guidance of the principal, the dean of students, and other teachers and staff to be able to carry out proper activities. If middle school students are unwilling to be led by the principal, the dean of students, etc., and go to activities casually, the school should strictly correct them. The Education Bureau will definitely provide assistance for this kind of corrective sanctions, as long as it is reasonable and it is something that teachers and staff should do, the Education Bureau will definitely help teachers and staff to bring students into line. I think some schools are already doing this, and some schools are also definitely planning to do it, but I am afraid that many schools still do not understand the attitude of the Education Bureau, so the first point is to put forward this idea and make a sincere hope and request to everyone. For the sake of middle school students, for the sake of the entire society, and for the sake of the future of the nation, we must hurry up and take this responsibility. If we do not find this line of defense very firmly, I am afraid that the phenomena seen in universities in the past few years may affect middle schools in the future. If it once affects them, then the damage to society and the nation, the magnitude of the crime, will be even more serious than that of universities. The incurable consequences in the future will definitely exceed our expectations.

Second, the guiding principles for training middle school students in the future. Each school must have a plan to train and guide students now. Today, I would like to contribute a method for your reference, that is, to implement the outline of the New Life Movement. The method formulated by the Education Bureau is only an outline. The implementation details of this method still need to be formulated in detail by each school. The various words of the New Life Movement only contain all the reforms that should be made in various daily life activities, and they are very common and not novel and outstanding. If there is no slogan or method for the New Life Movement, if the schools train students well, they are implementing the New Life Movement anytime and anywhere. However, of course, there are many places where everything can be done to achieve twice the result with half the effort. We seize this opportunity and grasp this New Life Movement as an outline for training students, and we will definitely be able to achieve great results. However, although the New Life Movement is a common thing, if it is not done well and the name is borrowed, it will be counterproductive. It seems that the name and content of the New Life Movement are indeed very good and should be done in this way. If school teachers and staff and public officials do not think of ways to implement it, then this movement will have no results. To implement it, we must teach people to implement it first. One type is public officials, and the other type is school teachers and staff. These two types of people must use their own implementation to influence ordinary students. Students in school are studying, and in the family and society, they can influence others. It can be seen that the relationship of the school is significant. Therefore, schools must implement the New Life Movement effectively, Ningke will do it step by step, and do not hope to do everything well in one day. This method is only prescribed in the outline by the Education Bureau. The implementation steps must be determined by each school according to the environment. Each school hopes to handle the details of the plan in phases. When handling it, we must pay attention to the teachers and staff themselves, so that the teachers and staff can promote the students. Therefore, the implementation method of the New Life Movement in primary and secondary schools does not hope that students will be allowed to do it indiscriminately in the absence of guidance in the name of the New Life Movement. We must attach importance to doing it, and we do not want an empty frame. The so-called empty frame is like organizing branches, conducting elections, taking pride in being an elected official, and even cleverly setting up names to compete with each other. To be honest, the New Life Movement in primary and secondary schools is the training of students, and it is what schools should train students in at that time. Students should not be allowed to run on the wrong road by themselves, and the name of the New Life Movement should not be used as a stepping stone for other activities, and absolutely cannot let this kind of person who goes the wrong way spread. Teachers and staff must resolutely stand up to take this responsibility. Training by teachers and staff will definitely reduce errors and complete the New Life Movement. This is the second point of hope. What you principals and deans of students are responsible for is not only the principals and deans of students, that is, all teachers and staff should also be responsible. At present, some people in the school think that guiding students is only the responsibility of the training staff or the principal, and that teachers can be irresponsible. I hope that everyone will change this atmosphere and make all teachers and staff in each school understand that leading and training students is the responsibility of every teacher, not the responsibility of any one person. We believe that the power of good teachers and staff in schools is greater than that of others, so we can know that if you want the school spirit to be good and the student discipline to be good, you must pay the same attention when hiring teachers. In this way, the school spirit can be good. In addition to setting up methods for the New Life Movement, the most important center of gravity must be placed on the teachers and staff. Teachers and staff should lead by example. If students do something wrong, they must be corrected. I hope that each school will implement it as soon as possible. The Education Bureau will send people to inspect it at any time in the future.

The third point I want to report on this occasion is about teaching affairs. Shanghai has held two joint examinations. Recently, the Ministry of Education has promulgated new regulations, and graduates of normal schools should also take the joint examination. The Education Bureau has asked the Ministry of Education to postpone this for one semester. The reason is that time is tight. When the Ministry of Education promulgated this regulation, some normal schools had already taken the examination, and some school students were visiting. I am afraid that it will be delayed, so we request a postponement. As for senior high school general subjects and junior high school, they will still be held, and primary schools will still not be held. The subjects of the middle school joint examination are stipulated by the Ministry of Education, and the methods will follow the past situation and be appropriately formulated.

Because of the joint examination, I thought of a subject problem. The purpose of the joint examination is, on the one hand, to make the level of middle schools more uniform, and on the other hand, to make students pay more attention to the curriculum. However, we cannot completely achieve the purpose of uniformity of degrees by relying solely on the joint examination. Therefore, we are now considering how to make the teaching level of each subject more uniform. Now each school has its own special situation. Some schools are good at Chinese, some value English more, and some are good at mathematics and science. Only by thinking about making the teaching progress of each subject in each school have a uniform method can the Education Bureau now plans to compile a progress chart for each subject, each grade, and each semester based on the curriculum standards of the Ministry of Education. This chart cannot be compiled solely by the staff of the Education Bureau, for fear that difficulties will arise in practice in the future. Therefore, we hope to cooperate with the school to formulate a relatively applicable chart. The Education Bureau has notified each school to help and recommend outstanding teachers with experience and research in each subject to jointly compile this teaching progress chart for each subject in middle schools in Shanghai. This work is planned to start in late May and be completed in early September, with a preparation time of three and a half months. After the chart is compiled, it will be distributed to each middle school for trial implementation. It is hoped that from the first semester of the 23rd year, the level of students in each class will follow this chart. Although it cannot be fully achieved at once, after one or two years, it will gradually achieve a more uniform level. The Education Bureau will send people to each school at any time to investigate. This chart will be used as a standard and should not be too fast or too slow, so that senior high school general subjects and junior high school have a uniform pace, and there is no phenomenon of differences in each subject. We hope that everyone will help with this work. If you have any comments, you can report them to the Education Bureau at any time.

Secondly, it is hoped that the teachers and staff in middle schools should preferably be full-time and less part-time, because if we want to hope that teachers will lead students, it is impossible for part-time teachers. Furthermore, in the future, whether it is a public or private school, the administrative aspects of exchange and research group activities should be borne by the principal, dean of students, and dean of teaching. In addition, there should be more teachers and staff, and their thoughts, abilities, and time should be used within the school, and they should no longer specialize in running outside the school. There is a slogan, that is, "School teachers and staff should go to school." If ordinary teachers and staff focus on teaching, students will not neglect their studies. This important point, I am willing to plead for middle school students to teachers and staff.

In conclusion, in the middle school, whether it is training in subjects or group activities, we hope that teachers and staff will take on major responsibilities. We want to make ordinary teachers and staff take on the responsibility of training in addition to teaching. The Education Bureau will closely cooperate with each school in the future and conduct investigations at any time. I hope that each school will help the Education Bureau to realize the progress of middle school education in Shanghai.

Ruan Lue, Director of Military Training at Jiaotong University, Resigns and Travels East

Ruan Lue, Director of Military Training at National Jiaotong University, has been in office for many years. He was hired by the Commercial Press to compile and print the book "Military Education," which has already been published. Recently, in order to pursue further studies, Mr. Ruan has resigned from his position and accompanied his wife, Ms. Bai Dingzhang, to Japan for studies on the Shanghai Maru at 9:00 am yesterday morning. More than 30 of his friends, including Zhang Liquan, Ma Xiezhong, Song Chongjiu, Pan Tinggan, Jiang Zhennan, Zhang Zhengguang, You Yigao, Ms. Huang Dequan, and Miss Yi Chonghua, saw him off at the Wusong Wharf. It is said that Mr. Ruan will engage in the study of political law after arriving in Japan, and he will be able to make many contributions when he returns to the country in the future. It is said that Ruan Lue, whose courtesy name is Xiaojun, is 28 years old and is from Wengan County, Guizhou Province. He graduated from the Sericulture Department of Guizhou Provincial Agricultural College and the Artillery Department of the Central Military Academy. He has served as a secretary, adjutant staff officer, regimental adjutant, and military instructor in middle schools and universities in the Yunnan-Guizhou Army. General Meeting of the China Education Construction Society: Teng Yangzhi's Report on His Observations and Reflections on Japanese Education; Decision Made on the Research Focus for the Next General Meeting

The China Education Construction Society held a general meeting of its members at Guangxia Middle School the other day. Teng Yangzhi reported on his observations and reflections on Japanese education. Several important matters were discussed and resolved. The details are as follows:

Attending Members

A total of more than 20 members attended, including Huang Yangyu, Sun Yuanzeng, Li Xuefeng, Xu Wancheng, Tan Tengfang, Liu Yiqing, Zeng Yanhua, Wang Jinyi, Chen Jingyu, Teng Yangzhi, Wang Yunshi, Gao Zhisheng, Zhang Zhonghuan, Lu Shaoji, Cheng Kuanzhi, Wu Zhiqian, Li Chao, etc. Sun Yuanzeng chaired the meeting, and Gao Zhisheng and Cheng Kuanzhi served as secretaries.

Observation Report

First, Teng Yangzhi reported on his observations and reflections after inspecting Japanese education: (1) From a social perspective, the entire Japanese society, from the government to the general public, focuses on the idea of ​​invading China. The general level of the Japanese people is relatively high. The number of people receiving compulsory education accounts for more than 99.5%. People are able to maintain order, pay attention to etiquette, and the three items of clothing, food, and housing are simple. Travel is convenient and smooth. The people of the whole country are working hard towards the general goal of "loyalty to the emperor and love for the country." Regarding the invasion of China, they generally believe that China's demise is inevitable, but Japan is wronged to be burdened by China's demise. Therefore, Japan should work hard to seize China.

Military Training

In terms of military training, the key points of school military training are (1) teaching by active-duty military officers, (2) practicing with real guns on the ground, and (3) treating students as soldiers. Military organs and educational organs are integrated. In addition, there is youth training, with elementary schools as the center and presided over by elementary school principals. In-service soldiers are trained with a martial spirit, with strict organization, encouraging people to die for the public, valuing practicality and not focusing on appearances, and doing things in a down-to-earth manner. Those who take public office are willing to take responsibility.

Education

The teaching methods are simple and lack change. The teaching materials are issued by the Ministry of Education and are consistent across the country and are very simple, but students learn a lot because the supplementary materials are rich. Students' learning attitude emphasizes spirit, and they pay special attention to physical education. The equipment is very complete and focuses on experiments. Teachers are secure in their jobs and rarely change jobs. Strictly speaking, Japanese culture does not have a national culture of Japanization. In the old aspect, it absorbs Chinese culture, such as loyalty, filial piety, and Shinto teaching, which dominates the entire Japanese society. In the new aspect, it absorbs Western culture, such as researching science, applying science, and promoting mechanization and electrification.

Discussion of Proposals

After Teng's report, the proposals were discussed. (1) Regarding the proposal to visit the Huangdu Chicken Farm on a regular basis, it was decided to visit on May 20. (2) Regarding the proposal to assign members to collect the Huangdu Chicken Farm shares, it was decided to assign Sun Kangzeng, Liu Yiqing, and Zhang Zhonghuan to be responsible for the collection. (3) Regarding the proposal to collect old shares and solicit new shareholders on a regular basis, it was decided to collect all shares before May 15. (4) Regarding the proposal to determine the research focus of the next general meeting of members, it was decided that how to train young people should be the research focus of the next general meeting of members, and Teng Yangzhi, Sun Kangzeng, Lu Jishao, and Zeng Chang were requested to conduct preliminary research and submit a written report at the general meeting. After the discussion, the meeting adjourned.

Xinfeng Foreign Bank reported that the New York stock market yesterday (the 10th) broke the low record of this year. The small exchange and the stock exchange were slightly the same, and the prices of securities were generally low. However, American public bonds created a new peak this year. It was heard that banks, insurance companies, and private individuals bought them because they had confidence that the government would eventually adopt a conservative fiscal policy. According to the agent's report, (securities) suffered two severe sell-offs, which were heard to be largely from professional speculators. The recovery at the end was still good, and it seemed that it would be mixed for the time being, but it would be easy to rise if there was good news. (Wheat) There was a large dust storm, and the public participated in a surge, predicting that the price would rise significantly. North America is currently suffering from a severe drought. (Cotton) The market was mediocre, waiting for the silver plan, and the foothold was firm. (Rubber) It fell in the early morning due to the impact of Singapore and London.
